<title>Document</title></head><body><div id="i75cae51fe15b4aa884dd10afba41f604_1"></div><div style="min-height:86.4pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">News Release </font><font style="color:#98ca3c;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">I</font><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> For Immediate Release</font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Georgia',serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">FactSet Reports Solid Results for Second Quarter 2021</font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Georgia',serif;font-size:14pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Revenue increases 6% and EPS rises 9% </font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Georgia',serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">NORWALK, Conn., March&#160;30, 2021 - FactSet (&#34;FactSet&#34; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) (NYSE&#58;FDS) (NASDAQ&#58;FDS), a global provider of integrated financial information, analytical applications, and industry-leading service, today announced results for its second quarter ended February&#160;28, 2021. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Second Quarter Fiscal 2021 Highlights</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Revenue increased 6.0%, or $22.0 million, to $391.8 million compared with $369.8 million for the same period in fiscal 2020. The increase is primarily due to higher sales of analytics and content and technology solutions (CTS).</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> Organic revenues grew 4.9%</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> to $389.2 million during the second quarter of fiscal 2021 from the prior year period. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) plus professional services was $1.6 billion at February&#160;28, 2021, compared with $1.5 billion at February&#160;29, 2020. The organic ASV plus professional services growth rate, which excludes the effects of acquisitions, dispositions, and foreign currency movements, was 5.5%. The primary contributors to this growth were higher sales of research and CTS solutions offset by lower sales of analytics solutions. Please see the &#8220;ASV + Professional Services&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Operating margin increased to 29.6% compared with 28.7% for the same period last year. Adjusted operating margin improved to </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">32.6% compared with 31.8% in the prior year period primarily as a result of reduced employee-related operating expenses due to the coronavirus pandemic.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share (EPS) increased 8.7% to $2.50 compared with $2.30 for the same period in fiscal 2020. Adjusted diluted EPS rose 6.7% to $2.72 compared with $2.55 in the prior year period primarily driven by an improvement in operating results partially offset by a higher tax rate. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">The Company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the second quarter increased to 15.7% compared with 14.0% a year ago, primarily due to lower windfall tax benefits from stock-based compensation compared with the three months ended February&#160;29, 2020.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">The Board of Directors of FactSet approved an increase of $206 million to the Company's existing share repurchase program on March 23, 2021, bringing the total amount available for repurchase under this program to $350 million.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet has increased the lower end of its organic ASV plus professional services outlook to $70 million from $55 million. FactSet reaffirms other metrics of its annual outlook for fiscal 2021. Please see the &#8220;Annual Business Outlook&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> </font></div><div style="padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8220;I am proud of how we executed this quarter, resulting in a solid first half of our fiscal 2021,&#8221; said Phil Snow, CEO, FactSet. &#8220;In our second quarter we saw a number of key wins validating our strategy for long term growth. Our focus on digital transformation, content expansion, and being an open platform continues to resonate with our clients as they navigate a rapidly evolving landscape.&#8221;</font></div><div style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8220;Our sustained cost discipline, productivity and continued execution of our investment plan have resulted in solid operating results and allow us to raise the lower end of our full-year organic ASV range to $70 million from $55 million,&#8221; said Helen Shan, CFO, FactSet. &#8220;We enter our fiscal second half with good momentum and remain focused on delivering significant value to our clients and shareholders.&#8221;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) + Professional Services </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV at any given point in time represents the forward-looking revenues for the next twelve months from all subscription services currently supplied to clients. Professional services are revenues derived from project-based consulting and implementation.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV plus professional services was $1,598 million at February&#160;28, 2021. Organic ASV plus professional services was $1,593 million at February&#160;28, 2021, up $83.5 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 5.5%. Organic ASV, which excludes the effects of acquisitions, dispositions, and foreign currency movements, plus professional services, increased $35.0 million over the last three months. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates for the second quarter of fiscal 2021 were 5.5% and 6.3%, respectively. Buy-side clients accounted for approximately 84%</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> of organic ASV while the remainder was derived from sell-side firms that perform mergers and acquisitions advisory work, capital markets services, and equity research. Supplementary tables covering organic buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates may be found on the last page of this press release. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Segment Revenue and ASV</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Americas region was $985.2 million compared with the prior year period of $925.6 million. Organic ASV increased 5.9% to $980.3 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Americas revenues for the quarter increased to $248.0 million compared with $232.7 million in the second quarter last year. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months, the Americas region organic revenue growth rate was 5.8%. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:7pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">2</font></div><div style="padding-right:18pt"><font style="color:#dcdcdc;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:6pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:86.4pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">News Release </font><font style="color:#98ca3c;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">I</font><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> For Immediate Release</font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the EMEA region was $427.6 million compared with the prior year period of $407.9 million. Organic ASV increased 3.7% to $426.8 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">EMEA revenues were $105.5 million compared with $102.1 million from the second quarter of fiscal 2020. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the EMEA region organic revenue growth rate was 1.5%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Asia Pacific region was $159.8 million compared with the prior year period of $146.1 million. Organic ASV increased 9.1% to $160.4 million. Asia Pacific revenues were $38.3 million compared with $34.9 million from the second quarter of fiscal 2020. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the Asia Pacific region organic revenue growth rate was 8.7%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Segment ASV does not include professional services, which totaled $25.0 million at February&#160;28, 2021.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Operational Highlights &#8211; Second Quarter Fiscal 2021</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Client count as of February&#160;28, 2021 was 6,103, a net increase of 164 clients in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in wealth management and corporate clients. The count includes clients with ASV of $10,000 and above.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">User count increased by 6,659 to 153,355 in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in wealth advisory users. The Company has changed the methodology for its user count. FactSet now includes users across all its products including workstations, StreetAccount and other workflow solutions. Revised historical user counts have been provided on the last page of this press release.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Annual ASV retention was greater than 95%. When expressed as a percentage of clients, annual retention improved to 90%, year over year. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Employee count was 10,660 as of February&#160;28, 2021, up 7.8% over the last twelve months. Excluding the Truvalue Labs acquisition, headcount grew by 7.4%, primarily driven by increased hiring in the Company's content and product development organizations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Net cash provided by operating activities increased to $140.7 million compared with $99.7 million for the second quarter of 2020. Quarterly free cash flow increased to $130.2 million compared with $74.6 million a year ago, an increase of 74.7%, primarily due to improved working capital from timing of tax payments and lower capital expenditures.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Capital expenditures decreased to $10.4 million, compared with $25.1 million a year ago, primarily due to reduced capital outlay for construction costs. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">A regular quarterly dividend of $29.1 million, or $0.77 per share, was paid on March&#160;18, 2021, to holders of record of FactSet&#8217;s common stock at the close of business on February&#160;26, 2021. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#4b4b4b;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">FactSet was selected by the Royal Bank of Canada (RBC) as their primary market data and technology provider for their entire wealth management organization. The Company will deploy its web-based wealth workstation and a suite of leading content sets to over 8,000 RBC wealth management professionals.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">The Company continued to make inroads in the environmental, social and governance (ESG) market through enhanced offerings. FactSet launched the Truvalue Labs&#174; SDG Monitor, designed to enable investors and other interested parties to view the alignment of corporations around the globe to the UN Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) in real time. Additionally, FactSet announced a joint offering with Ping An Insurance (Group) Company of China for investors considering ESG metrics for companies incorporated in China. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">FactSet expanded its open and connected data solutions by integrating its exclusive FactSet Concordance Service into Snowflake's cloud, allowing clients to connect FactSet, third party, and proprietary data. Additionally, the Company developed an application for financial news and data for Microsoft Teams, the business communications and collaboration platform developed by Microsoft.</font></div><div
